//QC - Defect no 26106
var _hddata = new Object();

var persistentCookieExpireL = 2592000000;
var wcPersistent = readBrowserCookie('WC_PERSISTENT');
var wcUserActivity = getUserIdFromUserActivityCookie();

var status = "";
var userId = "";
//Authenticated user
if(readCookie("THD_USERSTATUS") == "1"){
	status = "authenticated";
	userId=	wcUserActivity;
}//Recognized user
else if(readCookie("THD_REMEMBERME") && readCookie("THD_USERSTATUS") != "1"){
		status = "recognized";
		userId= wcUserActivity;
}
else if(wcUserActivity==-1002)
{
	//Default status is anonymous
	status = "anonymous";
	userId = "-1002";
}
else
{
	// Guest
	status = "guest";
	userId= wcUserActivity;
}
_hddata["custStatus"]= status;
_hddata["customerID"]=userId;

var experienceType = readCookie('THD_ONLINE_CHANNEL');

if(experienceType == 'E1=S3'){
	_hddata["experienceType"]="tablet";
}else{
	experienceType = readCookie('THD_USERTYPE');
	if(experienceType == 'P'){
		_hddata["experienceType"]="pro";
	} else{
		_hddata["experienceType"]="consumer";
	}
}
</script>

function findCategoryUrl(url1){

<script language="javascript">
	getLocalStore();
	var test = "";	
	function removeUrlHead(sUrl) {   
		var sString = sUrl.substring("//"+2);
		var pos = sString.substring("/"+1);
		sUrl=sUrl.substring(pos);
		return sUrl; 
	}

	function removeBrowseOption(sUrl) {
		var url = sUrl.toString();
		if(url.indexOf("&browsestoreoption=0") != -1) {
			url = url.replace("&browsestoreoption=0", "");
		}
		if(url.indexOf("&browsestoreoption=1") != -1) {
			url = url.replace("&browsestoreoption=1", "");
		}
		if(url.indexOf("&browsestoreoption=2") != -1) {
			url = url.replace("&browsestoreoption=2", "");
		}
		if(url.indexOf("&browsestoreoption=") != -1) {
			url = url.replace("&browsestoreoption=", "");
		}
		return url ;
	}
   
	function submitFormToLocalize(browseInfo) {
	    document.getElementById('sff').action = "http://www.homedepot.com/webapp/wcs/stores/servlet/THDPlsLocalize?storeId=10051&amp;langId=-1&amp;catalogId=10053";
	    var aStr = removeUrlHead('' + document.location);
	    document.getElementById('sff').redirect.value = aStr;
	    document.getElementById('browseStoreInfo').value = browseInfo;
		document.getElementById('sff').submit();
	}

   	function onlineOnly() {
		//cookieManager.createCookie('THD_NAVLOCALSTORE','0',null);
		//cookieManager.createCookie('THD_NAVONLINESTORE','8125',null);
	    var redirect = document.location;
	    redirect = removeRecordCompare(redirect);
		redirect= removeBrowseOption(redirect);
		document.location = redirect+"&browsestoreoption=0";
	}
   
   	function storeOnly(localized) {
		//cookieManager.createCookie('THD_NAVONLINESTORE','0',null);
		var redirect = document.location;
		redirect = removeRecordCompare(redirect);
		if (localized) {
			redirect= removeBrowseOption(redirect);
			document.location = redirect+"&browsestoreoption=1";
		} else {
	   		submitFormToLocalize("1");
		}
	}
   
	function onlineAndStoreSFL(localized) {
		//cookieManager.createCookie('THD_NAVONLINESTORE','8125',null);
		var redirect = document.location;
		redirect = removeRecordCompare(redirect);
		if (localized) {
			//cookieManager.createCookie('THD_NAVLOCALSTORE',window.locStoreNo,null);
		   	redirect= removeBrowseOption(redirect);
			document.location = redirect+"&browsestoreoption=2";
		} else {
    		submitFormToLocalize("2");	
		}
	}
</script>

<script language="javascript">
   function onlineAndStore(localized) {
	cookieManager.createCookie('THD_NAVONLINESTORE','8119',null);
		var currentBrowserURL = "";
	if (localized) {
		cookieManager.createCookie('THD_NAVLOCALSTORE',window.locStoreNo,null);
    		currentBrowserURL = document.location.href;
    		currentBrowserURL = removeBrowseOption(currentBrowserURL);
    		currentBrowserURL = currentBrowserURL + "&browsestoreoption=2";
	} else {
    		currentBrowserURL = getRedirectUrlForStoreFinder(true, true, '2', false);
			currentBrowserURL = "/StoreFinder/index.jsp?URL=" + currentBrowserURL;	
	}
		document.location.href = currentBrowserURL;
   }
	
   $(document).ready(function() {
   var ids=$("#certonaProductIds").val();
   if(typeof resx !== "undefined"){
	   	resx.links=ids;
	   	var refinement="Refinement_";
	   	if(! resx.rrqs) {resx.rrqs='';}
		else{// remove existing refinments
			var ttt= resx.rrqs.split('&');
			var original='';
			for(var t in ttt){
				if (ttt[t].indexOf(refinement)<0){
				original=original+ttt[t]+'&';
			}
			}
			original=original.replace(/&+/g,"&");
			resx.rrqs=original;
		}
		/* get all selected refinment and send only to certona.
		Refinement_Brand          
		Refinement_Color
		Refinement_Rating
		Refinement_Price      
		*/
	   	if(PLPModule !== undefined && PLPModule.Controller && PLPModule.Controller.checkboxStates){
		   for(var c in PLPModule.Controller.checkboxStates){
				refDetails = $("#"+PLPModule.Controller.checkboxStates[c]).val().replace("_s_","=");
				var nameValue = refDetails.split('=');
				if(nameValue && nameValue.length > 1 ){
				var refine= nameValue[0].toLowerCase();
				if(refine.indexOf("brand")>=0){
					refine="Brand";
				}else if(refine.indexOf("color")>=0){
					refine="Color";
				}else if(refine.indexOf("rating")>=0){
					refine="Rating";
				}else if(refine.indexOf("price")>=0){
					refine="Price";
				}else{ // ignore and continue on next item in loop.
				 continue;
				}
				var t2= refinement+refine+'=' +nameValue[1]+"&";
				if(resx.rrqs != null && ! resx.rrqs.indexOf(t2)>=0){
				 	resx.rrqs+=t2;
				}
				}
			}
			if(resx.rrqs != null){resx.rrqs=resx.rrqs.replace(/&+/g,"&");}
		}
		if(typeof certonaResx !== "undefined"){
			certonaResx.run();
		}
		}
	    //console.log("sa > ids:" + ids + "\n refs:" + refs);
		    //Reload the Ads after Ajax call
		    if ((typeof construct_google_csa_request !== "undefined") && (typeof google_csa_request_done !== "undefined")) { 
	    			var googleEnabled = true;
		    		if( googleEnabled === true) {
		    			var page = "PLP";
			   			var googlePropObj = {'adsafe' : 'high','adPage' : '1','channel' : 'TOOLS_%26_HARDWARE','hl' : 'en','adtest' : 'off','query' : 'Tools & Hardware  Specialty Tools  Auto Accessories  Truck Boxes ','pubId' : 'homedepot-browse_js'};
						var leftAdBlock = { 'container' : 'googleAdSenseLeft' , 'number' : '6' , 'adLoadedCallback' : google_csa_request_done , 'linkTarget' : '_blank', 'colorTitleLink' : '666666', 'colorText' : '666666', 'colorDomainLink' : '666666', 'colorBackground' : 'none', 'colorBorder' : 'none' };
						var bottomAdBlock = { 'container' : 'googleAdSenseBottom' , 'number' : '6' , 'adLoadedCallback' : google_csa_request_done , 'linkTarget' : '_blank', 'colorTitleLink' : '666666', 'colorText' : '666666', 'colorDomainLink' : '666666', 'colorBackground' : 'none', 'colorBorder' : 'none' };
						construct_google_csa_request(page, googlePropObj, bottomAdBlock, leftAdBlock);
   }
			}		
	   		
   });
   
   /**
    * The replace function will replace # with /, so that the store finder will redirect back to PLP
    * page after store localization.
    */ 
   function constructStoreFinderUrlForPLP() {
		var storeFinderRedirect = getRedirectUrlForStoreFinder(true, true, '2', false);
		window.open("http://www.homedepot.com/webapp/wcs/stores/servlet/StoreFinderView?storeId=10051&langId=-1&catalogId=10053&URL=" + storeFinderRedirect, '_self');
   }

<script language="javascript">	
if (document.URL.lastIndexOf('recordCompareList') != -1){
	var recordCompareList = getParamValue('recordCompareList');
	if(recordCompareList !=null){
		var tobechecked = splitArray(recordCompareList); // consisted selected
		var chkArray = document.getElementsByName("product");
		for (var i=0; i<chkArray.length; i++) {
			for(var j=0; j<tobechecked.length; j++) {
				if(chkArray[i].value==tobechecked[j]) {
					chkArray[i].checked = "checked";
					break;
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
</script>

	if(recordCompareList !=null){

<script language="javascript">	
if (document.URL.lastIndexOf('recordCompareList') != -1){
	var recordCompareList = getParamValue('recordCompareList');
	if(recordCompareList !=null){
		var tobechecked = splitArray(recordCompareList); // consisted selected
		var chkArray = document.getElementsByName("product");
		for (var i=0; i<chkArray.length; i++) {
			for(var j=0; j<tobechecked.length; j++) {
				if(chkArray[i].value==tobechecked[j]) {
					chkArray[i].checked = "checked";
					break;
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
</script>

if (document.URL.lastIndexOf('recordCompareList') != -1){
	var recordCompareList = getParamValue('recordCompareList');
	if(recordCompareList !=null){
		var tobechecked = splitArray(recordCompareList); // consisted selected
		var chkArray = document.getElementsByName("product");
		for (var i=0; i<chkArray.length; i++) {
			for(var j=0; j<tobechecked.length; j++) {
				if(chkArray[i].value==tobechecked[j]) {
					chkArray[i].checked = "checked";
					break;
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
var fed_CIsecure="https://cts-secure.channelintelligence.com/7580145_test_landing.js";
var fed_CInonsecure="http://cts.channelintelligence.com/7580145_test_landing.js";
var fed_CIcart="https://cts-secure.channelintelligence.com/7580145_test_cart.js";

var fed_ciurl = document.location.href;
var fed_cartValidate;
fed_cartValidate = fed_ciurl.indexOf("OrderItemDisplayViewShiptoAssoc");
var fed_confValidate;
fed_confValidate = fed_ciurl.indexOf("OrderOKView");
var fed_scripttag = document.createElement('script');
if(fed_cartValidate > -1){
	fed_scripttag.src=fed_CIcart;
} else if ( fed_confValidate > -1){	
	fed_scripttag.src=fed_CIconfirmation;
} else if (window.location.protocol=="http:"){
	fed_scripttag.src=fed_CInonsecure;
} else if (window.location.protocol=="https:"){
	fed_scripttag.src=fed_CIsecure;
}
var fed_insertloc=document.getElementById('ciscript_bcf');
if (fed_scripttag.src){
	fed_insertloc.appendChild(fed_scripttag);
}
</script>
